  Fontconfig configuration is done via /etc/fonts/conf.avail and conf.d.

  Configuration via /etc/fonts/local.conf is still possible,

linguas="ar ca ca@valencia cs da de el en_GB eo es fi fr gl id it ja ko lv nb nl pt pt_BR ru sl sr sr@latin sv tr zh_CN zh_HK zh_TW "; \
for lang in $linguas; do \
  dir=/tmp/glabels/pkg/glabels//usr/share/locale/$lang/LC_MESSAGES; \
  /bin/sh /tmp/glabels/src/glabels-3.2.1/install-sh -d $dir; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo $dir/glabels-3.0.mo; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo as $dir/glabels-3.0.mo"; \
  else \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo $dir/glabels-3.0.mo; \
    echo "installing ./$lang.gmo as" \
	 "$dir/glabels-3.0.mo"; \
  fi; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo.m; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo.m $dir/glabels-3.0.mo.m; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo.m as $dir/glabels-3.0.mo.m"; \
  else \
    if test -r ./$lang.gmo.m ; then \
      /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo.m \
	$dir/glabels-3.0.mo.m; \
      echo "installing ./$lang.gmo.m as" \
	   "$dir/glabels-3.0.mo.m"; \
    else \
      true; \
    fi; \
  fi; \
done
